	warn('File was created by someone else. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/database/database_connectivity_diagram.png');
	$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/database/database_connectivity_diagram.png');
	$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/database/database_connectivity_diagram.png')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
	warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
	if (!@copy('plugins/database/database_connectivity_diagram.png', $backup_name)) {
		warn('Creation of backup failed');
	}
}

	warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/database/database_connectivity_diagram.png');

	warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/database/database_connectivity_diagram.png');
}

if (!is_file('setup/index.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: setup/index.php');
	writefile_3();
	if (!is_file('setup/index.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): setup/index.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('setup/index.php') != 'fa81b67837207c786c8901de7d360b2471eedac8') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): setup/index.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('setup/index.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of setup/index.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('setup/index.php') !== 'fa81b67837207c786c8901de7d360b2471eedac8') {
		if (@sha1_file('setup/index.php') !== 'a9db3245ce553af5d3e1ca5f13c77042d6907864') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: setup/index.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('setup/index.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('setup/index.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('setup/index.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_3();
		if (@sha1_file('setup/index.php') !== 'fa81b67837207c786c8901de7d360b2471eedac8') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): setup/index.php');
		}
	}
}

	warn('File could not be deleted: setup/doc/database_connectivity_diagram.drawio');
}

	warn('File could not be deleted: setup/doc/database_connectivity_diagram.png');
}

// Dir deleted: setup/doc
@rmdir('setup/doc');
if (is_dir('setup/doc')) {
	warn('Directory could not be deleted (was not empty?): setup/doc');
}


file_put_contents('oidplus_version.txt', "Revision 258\n");
